					category = shbb_tech
				}

			else = {

					}

						ship_hull_super_heavy = 1
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ABY_yamato_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					add_equipment_production = {
						equipment = {
							type = ship_hull_super_heavy_1
							creator = "ABY"
							version_name = "Hoshino Class"
						}
						name = "Hoshino"
						requested_factories = 1
						progress = 0.75
						amount = 1
					}
					add_equipment_production = {
						equipment = {
							type = ship_hull_super_heavy_1
							creator = "ABY"
							version_name = "Hoshino Class"
						}
						name = "Abydos"
						requested_factories = 1
						progress = 0.75
						amount = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
